US Socialist Presidential Candidate Announces Foreign Policy 58

▲ A dispatch from Kuo Min News Agency, Boston, dated the 29th: The Boston Foreign Policy Association of the United States, believing that the foreign policy of political parties is often overshadowed by domestic issues during election campaigns, invited the Socialist presidential candidate, Norman Thomas, today to speak on the party's foreign policy. Mr. Thomas stated that the party's policy is based on seeking world peace and proposed six points: (1) immediately recognize Soviet Russia so that all countries can freely discuss the proposed peace issues; (2) organize the war debt issue at the World Economic Conference; (3) complete and real world disarmament; (4) strictly prohibit the supply of military materials and money to all aggressor nations; (5) end American dollar diplomacy; (6) stop all military education. Mr. Thomas has been involved in the world peace movement for 20 years. During the European War, he strongly advocated conscientious objection and wrote books to explain his views. He served as the editor of the National Weekly, promoting world peace with all his strength.

Prussian Administrative Reform 59

Papen and Braun Hold Conflicting Views

President's Mediation Fails

▲ A dispatch from Havas, Berlin, dated the 29th: Today, Papen, in his capacity as Administrative Commissioner of Prussia, and Braun, in his capacity as Prussian Prime Minister, were summoned by Hindenburg. The President's meeting with the two men was intended to mediate between them. However, the meeting did not go well. Braun fully acknowledged the ruling of the Supreme Court of Leipzig, demanding that the Administrative Commissioner appointed by the federal government only exercise his powers to the extent necessary to maintain public order. Papen, on the other hand, insisted on preserving the Administrative Commissioner's full administrative powers in order to carry out reforms in the Prussian administration. Braun also protested against the federal government's treatment of the Prussian cabinet members on July 20th. In short, the President's meeting with the two men failed to mediate between them and ended inconclusively.

▲ A dispatch from Kuo Min News Agency, Berlin, dated the 29th: The Bavarian state government has filed a protest with Federal President Hindenburg, stating, "If the federal government decides to interfere with the administrative reform of the Prussian state, it would be a serious violation of the constitutional position of the states in relation to the central government and between the states." Therefore, Bavaria wishes the President not to make a hasty decision before consulting with the authorities of other states. It is feared that the state of Hesse will soon take similar action. After receiving Bavaria's letter of protest, Hindenburg ordered Prime Minister Papen to notify the Bavarian state government that their conclusions and fears were based on a misunderstanding, as the federal government's actions were entirely based on the prerogatives granted to the federal commissioner by the Supreme Court.

US Wheat Surplus Problem 60

Second in Importance Only to the Presidential Election

A Struggle to the Death with Canada in Sales Competition

▲ A dispatch from Kuo Min News Agency, Chicago, dated the 29th: The current price of wheat is even lower than it was during the reign of Queen Elizabeth I of England. Therefore, the United States and Canada are competing to sell their wheat before the harvests in Argentina and Australia in order to reduce surpluses and maintain wheat prices. This intense competition between the United States and Canada is a fight to the death. In the United States, the grain problem is second in importance only to the presidential election. Almost everyone is talking about the catastrophic drop in grain prices and speculating about the future. Whenever a price drop is telegraphed, it is accompanied by countless rumors. Some claim that Russia is facing famine and will buy American wheat, others say that China has agreed to buy more wheat than originally planned, and still others say that Canada has sent commissioners to China to negotiate the sale of grain. However, these rumors are often difficult to verify. The market situation is even more chaotic. Whenever the market price drops sharply at the opening, the bulls often sell off everything they own. Later, when rumors suddenly emerge, the bears, fearing that the market will rise, begin to cover their positions, and the closing price rises slightly. Today's wheat market is exactly the same. At one point, the December price fell to 40 and 7/8 cents, but eventually rebounded to 44 and 1/8 cents. However, according to statisticians, this price is equivalent to the lowest wheat price since the time of Queen Elizabeth I.

Danish Parliament Orders Dissolution 61

▲ A dispatch from Reuters, Copenhagen, dated the 29th: The King of Denmark today ordered the dissolution of the Lower House on November 15th.

The British Observer Advocates Moving the British Embassy to Shanghai 62

▲ A dispatch from Reuters, London, dated the 30th: The Observer today published an article by its special correspondent, strongly advocating that British diplomatic personnel in China should engage in more effective cooperation with consular personnel. The correspondent not only suggested that the personnel of the two departments in China should be closer but also suggested that consular personnel should be in constant contact with British industrial areas and British chambers of commerce. It is claimed that commercial and diplomatic affairs should be reorganized, with Shanghai as the central point. The correspondent believes that now is the most appropriate time to move the British Embassy to or near Nanjing. Regarding this, the correspondent suggested either building a temporary embassy on the vacant land within the British Consulate General in Shanghai, with the British Ambassador residing in the Consulate General's residence, or renting a suitable building in Shanghai and building a temporary embassy next to it. It is said that if this were the case, the British Ambassador would have to be involved in the Shanghai issue. The correspondent replied that it would be good for the British Ambassador to be in close contact with the British expatriates in Shanghai. This plan would also save the expense of the embassy guard in Beijing. Another solution would be for the British Ambassador to temporarily reside in the temporary premises prepared in Nanjing. However, this would be more expensive, as it would require finding new houses to accommodate the staff, while this would not be necessary in Shanghai. The correspondent also argued that Britain should cooperate with China, but this should not be confused with leniency. For example, the China Indemnity Fund Board of Trustees, because the agreement did not have sufficient provisions for verification and auditing, resulted in "unsatisfactory features." The correspondent also cited Sir Simpson's recent work in China as a good example of cooperation.

Unemployed and Starving People Gather in London 63

Directed by the Third International

▲ A dispatch from Havas, London, dated the 29th: Mr. Hannington, the communist leader who led the demonstrators here on Wednesday, told the Daily News that the order for 2,000 "hunger marchers" to gather in London was issued from Moscow, with the aim of organizing such movements on an increasingly large scale, so that the workers could eventually seize power. The Daily News also stated, "The 2,000 hunger marchers are divided into several groups, each led by a communist agitator, and the expenses of the demonstration are provided by the International Red Aid and similar organizations."

Important News

Zhang Fang Arrives in Jinan to Discuss Shandong Problems 64

▲ Rumors of Liu Zhennian's troops leaving Shandong by sea

▲ Han indicates willingness to withdraw defenses first if Liu leaves Shandong

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong problem has been delayed and unresolved. Chairman Chiang, considering the many years of friendship between 20th Route Army Commander Zhang Fang and Han Fuju, has specially sent him to Jinan to meet with Han to discuss a solution. Zhang arrived in Jinan by special train at 3:00 AM on the 26th, after departing from Hankou. He arrived in Kaifeng at 3:00 AM on the 27th. Because the Chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, Liu Zhi, was also very concerned about the Shandong incident, he sent a telegram inviting Zhang to meet in Kaifeng. Therefore, after arriving in Kaifeng, Zhang disembarked to meet with Liu. He departed from Kaifeng at 11:00 AM. Liu Zhi's representative, Liu Yaoyang, came along. At 8:00 PM, they arrived in Xuzhou. Liu Yaoyang disembarked due to some business. At 11:40 PM, they departed from Xuzhou northward. Today (the 28th) at 11:40 AM, they arrived in Jinan. Most of the important figures here, from Han Fuju downwards, had worked with Mr. Zhang in Henan for many years, so there were many people who came to the station to welcome him. They included Civil Affairs Commissioner Li Shuchun, Finance Commissioner Wang Xiangrong, Industry Commissioner Wang Fangting, Education Commissioner He Siyuan, Zhang Yue of the Provincial Committee, Cao Liqing, section chief of the Department of Construction in place of the ill Department head Zhang Honglie, Zhang Weicun, Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Li Wuchen, Director of the Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau, Gu Liang, Commander of the 22nd Division, Lei Taiping, Commander of the Handgun Brigade, Wen Chenglie, Mayor of Jinan, Wang Kairu, Chief of the Public Security Bureau, and others. Han Fuju arrived at the station last. When the special train arrived, the military band played loudly. Zhang Fang, Liu Yaoyang, and Zhang's secretary general, Feng Baiping, and secretary, Liu Xingjie, disembarked amidst a grand welcome. Zhang first greeted the welcomers with "You've worked hard," and then, pointing at the people with a smile, said, "You've all come to Shandong; only I'm left in Henan!" Han also laughed and said, "You're the reinforcements!" They laughed together and then left the station together in cars to rest at the Jiaoji Hotel. I immediately went to the Jiaoji Hotel to visit Zhang and was received. The following conversation took place: (Question) Commander, this mission is very important. What are the details? (Zhang answered) There is no special mission. Chairman Chiang is very concerned about the problem of Liu Zhennian's troops in Shandong. Because I have been friends with Chairman Han for many years, he asked me to come and take a look and meet with some colleagues and old friends. You could say it's half official and half private. (Question) What is the commander-in-chief's opinion on resolving the Shandong incident? (Answer) The commander-in-chief hopes for a peaceful resolution so that Shandong can return to peace and quiet. The commander-in-chief believes that Chairman Han is responsible for the security of Shandong. Therefore, the Shandong matter respects Chairman Han's intentions and has no specific preconceived notions. The goal is to ensure both the prestige of the central government and local security. (Question) It is reported that the central government has decided to transfer Liu Zhennian away from Shandong in order to quickly resolve the Shandong matter. Is this true? (Answer) The commander-in-chief's intention is to first stop military action so that the Liu Zhennian problem does not affect international diplomacy. As for transferring Liu away from Shandong, that is not a problem in itself. Don't overemphasize it. (Question) What are Han's views on this after the meeting with the commander? (Answer) How to proceed still requires detailed consultation with Chairman Han and instruction from the commander-in-chief before a decision can be made. I have not yet discussed Han's views. I will report back later. I also went to the provincial government to visit Han. According to him, he received a telegram yesterday from Director Tang (Xiang) of the Beijing Office, reporting that the central government had decided to transfer Liu's troops away from Shandong. Minister He (Yingqin) also sent a telegram, stating that he had decided to transfer Liu's troops away from Shandong and explaining the reasons and process of his telegram on the 19th (i.e., He's Hao telegram). Designating Yantai and Longkou as Liu's defense areas was to prepare for Liu's troops to leave Shandong from those two places in the future. The intention was very good. Vice Commander Zhang (Xueliang) sent a telegram, still advocating that Yantai and Longkou be temporarily garrisoned by a third party to facilitate Liu's transfer. I fully agree with this method because as long as Liu's troops leave Shandong, the suffering of the Shandong people will be relieved. I will comply with whatever. Now that the central government has decided to order Liu's troops to leave Shandong, the Third Route Army can withdraw first in order to resolve this matter as soon as possible. Zhang Boying (Fang) is here to discuss everything. However, Yantai and Longkou are inhabited by both Chinese and foreigners and are of great importance. It is best to order Commander Shen (Honglie)'s naval unit to be stationed temporarily in those two places so that they are familiar with the situation and no other accidents occur. One regiment of Ning's (Chunxiao)'s brigade of the provincial army currently stationed in Yantai and Li Xuande's cavalry brigade will arrive in Qixia today because there are Liu's defeated soldiers and bandits looting there, so they are going to suppress them. As for my resignation as chairman, it is because I feel that I lack political knowledge. Originally, when I took office as chairman two years ago, I only agreed to serve for one year. Now it has been more than two years, so I want to get rid of it. Chief Counselor Chiang (Bocheng) was the first person to mediate this matter. I ordered Director Liu (Xizhong) to go to Beiping and invite him to come to Jinan again so that everyone can discuss it together. Chiang telegraphed that he had already telegraphed the commander-in-chief for instructions and would arrive in Jinan in a day or two (note: Chiang telegraphed this afternoon, saying that he would arrive in Jinan early on the 29th). It is said that the central government may send a special commissioner to Shandong to supervise the withdrawal of the provincial army and to supervise Liu Zhennian's troops leaving Shandong by sea within a certain period of time. (28th)

The Situation of the Tianjin Tram Workers' Strike Intensifies 65

▲ Traffic in the Italian and French Concessions is Severed

▲ The Company Authorities Adopt a Tough Stance

Tianjin Correspondence: The workers of the Tianjin Tram and Electric Light Company, because their seven demands to the company were not met, went on strike on the morning of the 21st, and there is still no proper solution. Since the strike, all workers have been able to ride the trams without tickets, and passengers have been unusually crowded, making driving quite dangerous. The authorities of the Italian and French concessions, believing that this would disrupt traffic order, have not allowed trams to pass through the two concessions since the 25th, causing the people great suffering. On the Japanese concession side, only four trams were dispatched to carry passengers back and forth, but not outside the Chinese areas. The remaining trams were arranged by the municipal government and the union to operate around the walled city and from Beidaguan to Dongfuqiao to prevent traffic disruption and to prevent other incidents. Yesterday, the concession authorities, seeing that the strike had been prolonged and unresolved, protested to the municipal government, requesting that it be stopped quickly so that the situation could return to normal as soon as possible; otherwise, the concession authorities would also be affected by the company's reduced income and should be held responsible by the municipal government. Mayor Zhou Longguang has paid little attention to local affairs. After the strike occurred, in accordance with labor-management mediation regulations, he ordered the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Security Bureau to send personnel to mediate. Little did he know that tram and electric lights are the largest public utilities in Tianjin and are operated by foreigners. When the contract was originally signed with Yuan Shikai, the Minister of the Northern Seas during the Qing Dynasty, there were special preferential treatments that were not comparable to domestic Chinese-owned factories and companies. Therefore, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Director Li Ming, and the Public Security Bureau sent Section Chief Lu Wei to the company to mediate. The company not only refused to accept the workers' demands but also refused to mediate. Despite repeated persuasion, it was still ineffective. The two bureaus had no way to proceed and had to report the situation to the municipal government for review yesterday. The company's tough attitude is because it claims that it treats its workers very well. In February of this year, it gave everyone a raise. Usually, everyone takes two days off in rotation each month, and there are also seven public holidays, for a total of one month of rest each year. At the end of the year, everyone receives double pay, which is rare among other factories in Tianjin. Now that the workers have made demands, the company will not accept such insatiable greed, even at the cost of sacrifice. The only option is for the municipal government to stop the strike and protect the company's assets. Furthermore, when the company's board of directors met the other day, it also resolved to order the company to accept mediation. However, the board of directors is composed of directors hired by the company and appointed by the municipal government, including Chinese directors Zhou Longguang, Tao Jian, Shi Zizhou, and Zhang Ren, as well as Western directors Yan Huiqing, Zhang Boling, the manager of the Sino-Belgian Bank, and a certain Mr. Lin. They only have suggestions for the company and no power to make the company implement resolutions, which is completely different from ordinary boards of directors that hold real power. Therefore, all the company's operations, except for the company's general manager Wang Keshen's management, are telegraphed to the head office in Beijing for review in the event of special accidents. Currently, because the head office's reply and Wang Keshen's original intention are both unwilling to mediate, the strike is allowed to continue to spread, and the situation is becoming increasingly deadlocked. Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezong, seeing that the municipal government has not made efforts to mediate this strike, has again ordered and urged it to be handled quickly. In addition to sending personnel to pay attention to investigating the strike and encouraging the workers not to take extreme actions, the municipal party headquarters resolved at yesterday morning's regular meeting to send another letter to the municipal government, strictly ordering the company to accept the workers' demands to avoid the expansion of the situation. In the afternoon, Zheng Wei, Shao Hua, and Shi Zizhou were sent to meet with Mayor Zhou to discuss solutions. Currently, Mayor Zhou Longguang, due to pressure from all sides, has specially summoned Lin Zixiang, the Chinese Affairs Director of the company, and Deng Qinglan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, to the government to discuss solutions. The first step must be for the company to agree to mediate before the workers can be persuaded to resume work. As for the seven demands put forward by Xu, the company has not yet made any indication. The union believes that the seven conditions are very ordinary and hopes for a proper solution and is waiting for the authorities to mediate. (October 28)

Current Situation of the Fujian Provincial Defense Army 66

▲ Chen Weiyuan Dissolves He Xianzhu's Troops

▲ The 60th Division Advises Chen Guohui's Troops

Fuzhou Correspondence: After He Xianzhu, Deputy Brigade Commander of the Third Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, was arrested in Shantou, fellow villagers' associations from all over Southern Fujian requested that the Pacification Headquarters send personnel to escort him back to Fujian to be interrogated together with Chen Guohui. Mr. He was escorted from Shantou on the 24th and will arrive in Fujian within a few days. Xinghua people in Fuzhou and Xiamen are collecting evidence in preparation for presenting it at the interrogation. As for the Third Battalion of the Third Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, which was concurrently commanded by He Xianzhu, its troops, such as the Wang Kui, Zhang Yuanjing, Jiang Xiang, and Zheng Ying battalions, were all bandits from Putian and Xianyou counties and have been disbanded by the brigade commander Chen Weiyuan. Only the Chen Tongliang and Ji Chuan regiments remain, one stationed in Putian county town and the other stationed in the Hanjiang commercial port. After reorganization, they will depart from Shuitaikou at the end of the month and go to Minqing and Gutian to take on defense duties along the Minjiang River. The Huang Bingwu troops of the Fourth Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, originally stationed in Minqing and Gutian counties, have all moved to Pucheng to guard against the invasion of red bandits on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi border.

Chen Guohui's troops of the First Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army were defeated by the 19th Route Army in Xianyou. Led by Chen Peiyu, Commander of the Second Regiment, the remnants fled into the mountains bordering Dehua and Datian counties. Chen Peiyu is now in dire straits and has some regrets. In addition to Zhang Yan, Deputy Commander of the 61st Division, sending a letter to Chen, earnestly advising him to extricate himself and return, promising to preserve his life and give him an opportunity to rehabilitate himself and perform meritorious service, the 60th Division Headquarters also issued a proclamation, stating that if the soldiers of the brigade are willing to surrender, those who are foreigners can enlist in the local garrison of this unit and will be accepted. Those who are locals and have homes to return to will be given travel expenses of two yuan to escape and return home, and their self-employment will be protected in their hometowns to maintain peace and goodness. Those who return with weapons will also be rewarded as usual and will not implicate the innocent. However, when Chen's troops fled from Xianyou to Dehua, more than 2,000 guns were confiscated by the bandit Zhang Xiong'nan. The bandit, combined with the original guns, has a total of more than 3,000 guns, as well as many machine guns and artillery pieces. He occupies the Xishanshuikou area between Yongchun and Dehua and commits all kinds of evil. The 61st Division has sent troops to surround the area and force them to surrender their weapons and disband to avoid causing trouble in the area. (October 25)

Execution of Notorious Bandit Wei Baqun in Guangxi Province 67

▲ Shot to Death by Clan Nephew in Bandit Lair

▲ Head Severed and Sent to Military Department for Reward

Nanning Dispatch: Wei Baqun, the communist bandit who disturbed Donglan, Fengshan, and the Zuoyou Rivers, killing countless people, has been apprehended. Since returning to Guangxi from Hong Kong in the 13th year of the Republic [1924], he has been actively recruiting bandits and buying off ignorant peasants and Yao people. He consolidated his party, occupied Donglan, and carried out massive killings, placing the people in dire straits. Although government troops were dispatched to suppress him, the mountains were deep and the forests dense, and Wei's bandits relied on various caves stretching dozens of miles as natural defenses. As a result, despite years of suppression, they could not be completely eliminated. When Yu Zuobai returned to Guangxi in the 18th year of the Republic [1929], the tenacious bandits gained even more momentum, expanding their bandit army, burning and killing, causing extreme suffering. Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi repeatedly received telegrams from the people of Donglan and Fengshan, requesting the dispatch of troops to suppress the bandits and relieve the people from their suffering and stabilize the region. Therefore, last month, they ordered the 7th Army Commander Liao Lei to supervise capable troops and conscripted militias to suppress the bandits and alleviate the people's suffering. After receiving the order, Liao led a large army from Liuzhou, marching day and night towards Donglan and Fengshan. Upon reaching Donglan, he launched a large-scale encirclement of the bandit dens, capturing more than ten bandit strongholds, seizing hundreds of bandit guns and thousands of dan [unit of weight] of bandit grain. However, Wei's bandits continued to resist stubbornly. When Bai Chongxi inspected Donglan, he instructed Liao Lei on strategies for suppression and capture. All army groups then exerted their utmost efforts in searching and suppressing, and the people also worked hard in cooperation with the army groups. Finally, yesterday (the 19th), Wei's bandits were killed. Upon hearing the news, the people were overjoyed. Liao Lei and Guo Fenggang, the chief of staff of the army, and Ma Yongliang, the deputy adjutant sent by the headquarters, have successively telegraphed Li, Bai, and the provincial government to report. The telegrams are as follows:

(1) Telegram from Army Commander Liao (title omitted): "Upon investigation, the rebel Wei Baqun has incited rebellion in Donglan and Fengshan for more than a decade, and his disaster has spread to the Zuojiang River, with more than ten thousand people suffering from his tyranny. The tragedy is unbearable to witness. Troops have been dispatched to suppress him repeatedly, and I, Liao, have also come to Lan [Donglan] twice to suppress him, but I have failed to eliminate the main enemy and relieve your worries and eliminate the local disaster. This time, our Deputy Commander personally came to Donglan to instruct on strategies for suppression and capture. All units have searched and suppressed according to the law, and the people have worked hard. Relying on the power and virtue of the Commander and Deputy Commander, Wei Ang, a farmer from Dongli, with a deep understanding of righteousness, came out of the cave to surrender. Following the instructions given to him, he seized Wei Baqun's Mauser pistol in Shuangfa Cave near Dongli this morning (the 19th) and shot and killed Wei Baqun, severing his head and sending it to the headquarters for reward. After verification by the people of Wuzhuan, they unanimously confirmed that it was true. Furthermore, Liang Yixiang, a gentleman from Wuzhuan, had a close friendship with Wei Baqun since childhood. He witnessed the scene and stated that the head was indeed Wei Baqun's. Further investigation revealed that Wei Ang is Wei Baqun's clan nephew and was trusted by Wei Baqun, which is why he was able to kill him. After inquiring, it is confirmed to be true. I hereby telegraph to report for your inspection and approval." (Liao Lei, Hao Chen, seal) at Wuzhuan.

(2) Telegram from Chief of Staff Guo (title omitted): "According to the telegram from Deputy Adjutant Luo Minhao of this headquarters, 'The bandit Wei Baqun was shot and killed by farmer Wei Ang from Dongli in Shuangdong near Dongli Village this morning (the 19th), and his head was severed and sent to Wuzhuan. Further details will be reported later.' I hereby telegraph to report." (Guo Fenggang, Hao Xu, headquarters seal).

(3) Telegram from Deputy Adjutant Ma (title omitted): "The bandit Wei Baqun has ravaged Donglan and Fengshan, brutally killing compatriots, and his crimes are heinous. Our army has been suppressing him since the ninth month of the lunar calendar [October/November] . The bandit has been fleeing everywhere. He secretly sneaked into Dongli Shangfanong last night and fell asleep with a Mauser pistol under his pillow. He was robbed of the gun and shot to death by Wei Ang from the same village. At 7:00 AM this morning, Wei Baqun's head was sent to the Wuzhuan militia headquarters for verification. The people have confirmed that he was indeed killed. Remaining bandit leaders such as Chen Hongtao are currently being searched for by four police squads led by Wei Ang. Wei's bandit has now been executed, which is truly due to the power and virtue of the government and the fortune of Donglan and Fengshan. " (Ma Yongliang, Hao seal), (21st).

Anhui Provincial Party Affairs Commissioner Requests Increase in Import Tax on Foreign Rice 68

▲ And Requests the Abolition of Rice Permit Tax and Opium Public Sales

Wuhu Dispatch: Anhui Province has suffered from natural disasters and man-made calamities in recent years. The social economy has collapsed due to the instability of the rural areas, all industries are in decline, and the people's livelihood is withering. Chiang Kai-shek, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Three Provinces, previously sought to reverse the accumulated malpractices and encourage the people by issuing orders to all parts of the three provinces to strictly enforce the ban on opium. However, before a month had passed, the Hubei Special Tax Office suddenly sent personnel to Anhui to prepare for the public sale of opium. At that time, the Anhui Provincial Party Affairs Commissioner was ordered to inspect party affairs and traveled throughout the region. He witnessed widespread devastation and opium smoke everywhere, while the people's suffering was blocked from reaching the authorities. Therefore, he convened a meeting of party, government, and military leaders in Wuhu yesterday to discuss remedies. As a result, it was decided to telegraph to the central government, requesting it to order the Ministry of Finance to increase the import tax on foreign rice to raise the value of domestic rice. Another telegram was sent to the Anhui Provincial Government to abolish the Rice Grain Administration and the Rice Permit Tax, so that goods could flow freely and businesses could profit. Regarding the crackdown on opium public sales, a direct telegram was sent to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, requesting him to maintain the previous order and immediately order its abolition. The telegrams are recorded below:

▲ Telegram to the Central Party Headquarters: "Last year, Anhui Province suffered from a major flood, and the rural economy was on the verge of bankruptcy. This year, the autumn harvest has been completed, but the price of rice is low, and the farmers' suffering has deepened. Recently, the financial market has stagnated and cannot circulate, which has not only led to the decline of all industries and the impoverishment of the people, but also poses a hidden danger that may affect social stability. We were ordered to inspect party affairs in various counties and conducted a detailed examination of the situation in the rural areas, which was heartbreaking to witness, and our hidden worries are extreme. The underlying cause is the low price of rice and the financial hardship, while the low import tax on foreign rice, which floods the market, is the main reason for the decline in rice prices. If immediate relief is not provided, how can the people bear it? We hereby telegraph to your organization, earnestly requesting you to forward a letter to the National Government, ordering the Ministry of Finance to increase the import tax on foreign rice to raise rice prices, and to borrow a large sum of money from the Shanghai banking group to regulate the financial market, in order to maintain the people's livelihood and eliminate hidden dangers. We await your urgent orders."

▲ Telegram to Wu Zhongxin, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government (title omitted): "Lingyun et al. were commissioned by the Central Government to come to Wuhu to inspect party affairs. We have repeatedly heard from lower-level party departments and people's organizations that the establishment of a Rice Grain Administration in Wuhu to collect rice taxes is actually a disguised form of the old Rice Permit Tax. This kind of tax office disturbs merchants and harms the people, and the Central Government and the Ministry of Finance have already issued orders to abolish it. At a time when grain prices are low and rural areas are bankrupt, the imposition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies only exacerbates the suffering of merchants, and it hinders the smooth flow of goods. It not only affects the financial market, but also hinders the increase in rice prices. Therefore, we telegraph to your government, earnestly requesting you to deeply understand the people's feelings and immediately order its abolition to alleviate the people's hardship and maintain the financial market."

▲ Telegram to Chairman Chiang (title omitted): "Opium is harmful, weakens the country, and destroys the race. Your Excellency has repeatedly issued strict orders to ban opium and promulgated regulations for a limited period of time to quit opium. All our people should follow this instruction in order to completely eliminate opium. We were commissioned by the Central Government to come to Wuhu to inspect party affairs. We have repeatedly heard from lower-level party departments and people's organizations that Yang Youxin, a special commissioner sent by the Hubei Special Tax Clearing Office, has recently established an inspection office in Wuhu to collect special opium taxes. Such actions violate the ban on opium, openly collect taxes, not only violate the Premier's instructions, but also greatly betray your Excellency's strict ban on opium, and disregard laws and regulations. We hereby telegraph to your Excellency, urgently requesting you to immediately order its abolition and thoroughly investigate and deal with it. We await your urgent orders." (28th)

Representatives of Coal Industry in Jiangsu Counties Petition 69

Zhenjiang Dispatch: Today (30th) at 10:00 AM, all the coal industry representatives from the counties came to the provincial capital to petition. The provincial chamber of commerce representative Liu Zhanbai, the Zhenjiang chamber of commerce representative Zhao Xianbo led the provincial coal industry petition delegation representatives He Hefang, Ding Chonglian, Lin Zhisun, Zhang Yuqi, Yuan Junsheng, Huang Bofu, Ma Buzhou and other seven people and all county representatives, a total of more than one hundred and several ten people first went to the provincial government to petition. The Secretary-General Jin Baoguang received them on behalf of the government. The representatives stated their petition which was that formerly the tax rate for coal, rice and flour was the same, one per thousand. This time the rice and flour rate was revised to two per thousand while coal was increased to five per thousand and draught animals were increased fourfold. Merchants cannot bear this tax burden. Also, in this province Nanjing, Shanghai and other places have not increased the tax rate and the Shanghai concession has no obligation to pay taxes. The difference in production costs is too great and affects the coal sales. Also, the representatives analyzed in detail the relationship between coal and the people's livelihood is more important than rice and flour. Jin agreed to forward this to Chairman Gu and wait for review. The representatives then went to the Finance Department to petition. The Secretary Yu Juesheng received them and asked them why Jiangsu was using the same tax rate as Zhejiang but Jiangsu's coal industry felt it especially difficult. The representatives responded that Zhejiang has a lot of mountains and forests and is very rich in firewood. Except for the coal used in factories, most people use firewood as fuel, so Zhejiang's total coal sales in the whole year does not exceed one hundred thousand. The province of Jiangsu has factories everywhere and all use coal as a primary fuel, so the whole year requires three million dan. Recently, Japanese coal is being vigorously dumped and all sales of domestic coal has been occupied. If the tax rates are increased then it will be difficult for the coal industry to survive, please transfer the special difficulties of Jiangsu Province. Yu agreed to wait until the director returns to the office and personally give it to him. Then the delegation went to the Industry Department and Secretary Hou Junliu received them. The representatives stated their difficult circumstances and said that coal is a necessary product for all kinds of industries. If you want to revitalize the industry, you must reduce the cost of coal in order to enrich the production. Please provide as much relief as possible. Hou agreed to transfer to the Director for the representative to find a way to solve it. Then the delegation together went to the Provincial Party and Zhang, the committee member representative received them and enquired in detail the coal industry's difficulties. The party representatives said that the coal and the four major elements of people's livelihood has a close relationship and that rice and noodles only relate to one part of the four major elements of the people's livelihood. The tax rate is still two per thousand. Coal is more related to rice and flour yet the tax rate has suddenly increased four-fold. This is affecting the national economy and the people's livelihood and requested a way to provide relief. Zhang agreed to raise the issue at the party and government meetings for discussion and give full assistance. The representatives thanked them and left.

Important News Two

Yangqing Tax Riot Results in Six Executions by Firing Squad 70

▲ Provincial Committee Interrogation Determines They Were Principal Offenders

▲ Three Arrested for Colluding with Soldiers and Police at Jija Hotel

Yangzhou Dispatch: In the ninety-odd villages of the northwestern township of this county, incidents of burning houses have been discovered in recent days due to the Yangqing Tax Riot. Over the past two days, more than ten people have been arrested by the military and police and brought to the county. The two provincial committee members, Han Deqin and Li Mingyang, personally conducted strict interrogations. Six individuals, including Ge Guangxing (aka Ge Dayan), Chen Youxi (aka Chen Jintang), Luo Cailiang (aka Luo Pijiang), Yang Dechang, Liu Yushan, and Bu Dengyun, were identified as principal offenders. At 6:30 AM today (29th), Ge Guangxing and the other six were taken from the county government, their identities confirmed, and they were tied up and executed by firing squad outside the north gate near Longguang Temple. The charges were announced as follows: "It has been found that Jiangdu County has experienced incidents of gathering crowds and causing disturbances due to the investigation of field taxes. The Provincial Government has specially dispatched these commissioners to Yangzhou on the 25th to investigate and handle the matter. Over the past few days, we have repeatedly contacted and discussed with local figures, and the resolution of the Provincial Government's meeting on investigating field taxes pending further review has been announced. All blindly following offenders detained on the 23rd have been released on bail with leniency, and order has gradually been restored. However, on the 26th, a band of men suddenly gathered crowds, burned houses, and seized weapons in the northwestern townships. Military and police were dispatched to suppress the unrest, and several ringleaders who instigated and commanded the unrest were apprehended. It has been determined that they colluded with communist bandits, intending to take advantage of the opportunity to create chaos, which is unforgivable. They should be severely punished. In addition to Ge Guangxing, Chen Youxi, Luo Cailiang, Yang Dechang, Liu Yushan, and Bu Dengyun, whose testimonies are conclusive, being identified, verified, and executed by firing squad at the execution ground on the 29th of this month as a warning, the villagers in the other villages were coerced and blindly followed, and their circumstances are pitiful. These commissioners have reported to and been approved by the Provincial Government for general leniency and will not be pursued. They should all feel at ease, return home, and restore order. If anyone dares to fabricate rumors, gather crowds, burn houses, or seize weapons again, once verified, they will be arrested and charged as communist bandits and will not be spared. This proclamation is hereby urgently issued for the public to be informed." In addition, Chen Yongsheng and Chen Qiunian, whose circumstances were lighter, have been released on bail. Jiang Tingbao, Jiang Tingyan, and Jiang Tingkun are being held in custody by the Public Security Bureau. Last night, several thousand villagers gathered in the Jija Hotel area, attempting a riot. The 3rd Battalion of the Independent Regiment, led by Battalion Commander Wang, and the duty patrol team went to the scene to suppress the unrest. When their efforts proved ineffective, Battalion Commander Wang ordered the opening of fire, reportedly killing three people on the spot, injuring several, and arresting eight. The crowd dispersed. After interrogation by Battalion Commander Wang, three individuals, including Sang Rongjiu (village chief of the ninth district, one village), Hu Lazi, and Zhang Changxing, were found to be highly suspicious and were transferred to the county government by the police today. The other five individuals were released that night. This morning, the county detective team arrested Zhang Yuting in Hujia Square. It is reported that the villagers have dispersed somewhat. Director Li also transferred the security team stationed at Taiyang Palace to Ping Shan Tangzhen this afternoon to maintain order. Around 4:00 PM this afternoon, the two provincial committee members, Han and Li, invited reporters from this city to the River Works Bureau to make a statement, which was generally divided into the following points: (1) The causes and changes of the recent unrest (based on the interrogation results and what was personally witnessed by various parties); (2) The government must take decisive action (execution of principal offenders and release of offenders); (3) Measures to suppress the unrest in the future (still need to guide and appease); (4) The removal of the county magistrate (because County Magistrate Yang is unsuitable, he is planned to be removed in the shortest possible time); Hopes for the press: A, remain calm and do not amplify the propaganda; B, align the spirit with the government; Whether there is any corruption by the Yangqing tax personnel has not been verified at this time, but attention will be paid to it in the future, etc. It is reported that the county party headquarters convened a discussion with various people's organizations this afternoon, and the results decided: (1) Telegram to the Provincial Government, requesting that the two provincial committee members, Han and Li, be stationed in Yangzhou to maintain order until the Yangqing Tax Riot subsides; (2) Telegram to the Provincial Government, requesting an increase in troops to Yangzhou for defense. (29th)

Local Dispatch

Songjiang 71

▲ Songjiang Bank Directors Accused of Embezzlement: The Songjiang Bank collapsed this spring. After the president absconded, general depositors elected representatives to the procuratorate to accuse the bank's directors, Zhang Shengshan and others, of embezzlement and fraud. After an investigation by the procuratorate, all directors were released on bail. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, a continued investigation hearing was held. Only Zhang Xiaomei and Qian Xuanqing, the defendants, reported for duty. The plaintiff representatives, Bai Guanlan, Chen Nianci, and Wu Baohuang, all attended court and stated the embezzlement and fraud. According to the defendant's confession, all blamed the absconded president, Xie Liangda, to be responsible, "Although we are the bank directors we did not know the internal affairs." Then the prosecutor went with the plaintiffs, defendants and accountant Xia to the liquidation office to examine the bank accounts and at that time it was discovered that on February 5th, during the bank strike, the bank accounts had over 600,000 yuan of receipts and payments, which shows that this was bank fraud. Following this, the plaintiffs requested the prosecutor to file a public prosecution, so the bank would bear the responsibility to the depositors.

Wuxi 72

▲ Chen Yi Visits Wuxi to Survey Site for Nitric Acid Plant: He Yingqin, Minister of Military Affairs, recently proposed the establishment of a factory to manufacture and refine nitric acid. The factory site is planned to be located on Zhongshan Mountain in Taihu Lake, Wuxi, to avoid danger. A staff member was once sent to Wuxi to survey the site, but the matter was shelved due to funding and other issues. Recently, Chen Yi, Vice Minister and Director of the Ordnance Department, considered that the Sino-Japanese and January 28th incidents showed that nitric acid factories were necessary, so the former days he was accompanied by British consultant Gulao, chief technician Hong from the Ordnance Department, and secretaries and guards, a group of seven or eight people, to come from Beijing by car to Wuxi. They boarded a steamboat to the mountains of Taihu Lake and investigated the site in detail. Yesterday morning, they went to the mountains on the shore of the lake to conduct a survey, and also toured scenic spots such as Yuantouzhu and Xiaojishan. That night, they took an overnight train to Shanghai. Chief Technician Hong and the British consultant secretaries and adjutants took the 11:00 PM overnight train back to Beijing. It is said that after Chen returns to Beijing, he will draw up drawings and convene meetings for detailed discussion before a decision can be made.

▲ Xue Fengjie's Concubine Requests Division of Inheritance: Xue Wangruiying, the concubine of the late Xue Fengjie (also known as Long Guanzhu), filed a lawsuit with the county government, requesting a division of inheritance. Since Fengjie's death in the summer of the 19th year of the Republic of China [1930], his son, Daoqing, has failed to provide support payments. Fengjie has a total estate of over 400,000 yuan, according to regulations, she is entitled to 35,900 silver dollars. However, the county government has repeatedly held court sessions, but has not yet resolved the case. After the establishment of the County Court, Ruijing sued Daoqing for abandonment in the procuratorate, but the procuratorate decided not to prosecute the case. After two years of litigation, there was still no result. Most recently, Ruijing filed a lawsuit with the civil court, demanding that Xue Fengjie's wife, Qian, and his son, Daoqing, allocate funds for child support, education, and marriage. Yesterday was the date of the opening hearing of the case. The plaintiff, Xue Wangruiying, was present, and the defendant, Xue Daoqing, was present. Tang Ying, the plaintiff's agent lawyer, was also present in court. Judge Wang opened the trial. In addition to the plaintiff and defendant's statements of the case, lawyer Tang also made various points. After that, Judge Wang declared the debate of the case closed and scheduled the verdict for 2:00 PM on the 31st. The plaintiff and defendant were both ordered to return.

Nantong 73

▲ Tonghai Bandits to be Suppressed by Provincial Forces: Chen Diaoyuan, the first route commander of the provincial suppression of bandits, whose troops are suppressing bandits around Huaihai and Gaoyou, Tonghai bandits, are too far away, so he has requested the Military Committee to allow the provincial defense forces to suppress them. The provincial security office has been ordered to dispatch the first security regiment to take charge.

▲ Extension of Bandit Suppression Zone in Jiangxi for Six Months: The Jiangsu Higher Court has inquired whether twenty-seven counties, including Nantong, are still considered bandit suppression zones, to the Ministry of Defence for a decision by the Military Council. As there are still scattered bandits in the counties, the army should continue suppressing them separately. The term should be extended for six months. The counties have been informed.

Danyang 74

▲ Zhangyan Town Stores Robbed: More than 20 bandits carrying guns suddenly came to Zhangyan Town in the east township the other day, invaded the town, first fired guns to show their power, and then went to various stores to rob. The area's protection regiments responded to the police and fought with the bandits for a long time, driving the bandits back. Inspection of the stores showed huge losses. The protection regiment lost a box gun.

▲ Implementation of Land Survey in Urban Areas: Since the establishment of the county land bureau preparatory office, it has been actively working. The Provincial Land Bureau has dispatched the second squadron of the survey team to conduct a survey, and designated the urban area as the first area to be opened. The team leader Zhu Jiqun has led the entire team to Danyang to start the survey. County Magistrate Wang has ordered the town chief of the city area, Zhang, to instruct the town chiefs to lead and assist in the process.

Zhenjiang 75

▲ Jiangsu Reclamation Corps to Depart: In addition to the Yanken Company has collected sellers for the coastal wasteland in northern Jiangsu. There are also about 14 million mu of uncultivated land. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has selected Dongtai, Yancheng, Funing, and Lianshui to be reclamation zones. It has elected He Yushu and Leng Yuqiu to be preparatory members to first investigate the land, distinguish between official and private land, number of mu, soil quality grade, and plan surveying and water conservancy projects. This project is estimated to cost 20 million yuan per year for five years, for a total of 100 million yuan. Jiangsu's financial resources are exhausted and there is no extra funds to pay for it. It is reported that it has been decided that Rong Zongjing will borrow 100 million yuan from the United States. Recently, there has been hope for the completion of the loan. On the one hand, the provincial government is forming an investigation team. In addition to He Yushu, Li Mingyang, Miao Bin, Leng Yuqiu, and Dong Xiujia as natural members, the Ministry of Industry has also sent a representative, Pi Zuoqiong, to the province to participate. The team will depart within a few days, first to Nantong, Rugao, Yancheng, Dongtai, Lianshui, pass Xuzhou, and Haimen back to the province. The expenses required during the journey will be submitted to the provincial government for formal expenditure by the team in the future.

Yangzhou 76

▲ Robbers Commit Robbery and Murder: The home of She Fashan, a villager in the fourth village of Gongdao Bridge in the northern township of this county, was invaded by dozens of bandits the other day. They robbed the family and beat She's brother Youhan, sister-in-law Chen, and niece-in-law Chen to force them into giving money. Youhan's son, Yonghu, was beaten on the head and killed. The bandits fled around 9 PM last night. Yesterday (28th), She Fashan came to the city and went to the County Court and Public Security Bureau to report the incident and request an investigation.

Jiaxing 77

▲ Murder of Worker Case Arrests Perpetrator: Because a worker, Fu Youfu, from Xiaoshan who worked at Zhang Achang's farm in Huangjinqiao Jiaxing Yuqiao district had an affair with the mistress Xie the mistress lost her job, and unable to make a living, on the twenty-third night the worker dug through the wall and stole rice, then sneaked into the mistress' bedroom. Xie woke up in a dream and thought it was a thief, so she yelled for thief. Because of this the worker was arrested. Because of hatred Zhang Achang stuffed the worker's mouth with rags until it was full. At daybreak he saw the worker was already dead. Then Zhang hid the corpse in the river. On the twenty-eighth, the corpse was found in the river in Ma Jinqiao, Yuxian district. Some people identified the corpse as being Fu Youfu, who Zhang Achang had murdered. The fifth public safety bureau arrested Zhang Achang and Xie and sent them to the Jiaxing local sub-court for interrogation. The prosecutor went to examine the corpse on the thirtieth and then will schedule a hearing.

Xiaoshan 78

▲ Girl Murdered: On the twenty-seventh, the corpse of a girl of about ten years of age was found behind the bamboo forest temple on Chengqiaoxia Street, Dongmen, Xiaoshan. The local township office reported it to the court to send an official to examine it. At that time, the prosecutor Zheng Zhexin determined the girl was covered with red swelling, the skin beside the eyes was broken, there was a hole behind the head, and the blood was not dry. Zheng suspects that the girl had been beaten to death. Examining the clothes, she looks like a servant. When the examination was completed, Zheng ordered the police to investigate the matter within three days and report the situation for review. It is said that the maid was raised by a nearby resident, who abused her and abandoned her body in an empty lot after death. The county court is now investigating the truth of the case.

Educational News Highlights

Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools to be Promulgated Successively 79

It is reported that the Ministry of Education's curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools will be promulgated successively in the near future. This time, instructions and orders will be issued to the education bureaus of various provinces and cities to comply with the standards, rather than using a proclamation method. This is because the primary school part has been largely determined and will be promulgated first in the near future. The secondary school part, such as civics, is still being reviewed in detail and will be ordered soon. It is said that the standards of this session are not like the trial nature of the standards promulgated last year. Since they are officially decided standards, they must be adopted uniformly throughout the country. It is necessary to conduct thorough research in advance.

European Education Study Group's Itinerary 80

The Ministry of Education previously sent an European education study group led by Cheng Qibao, etc. They recently sent a letter to the Ministry of Education, outlining their study work in Poland. They are now scheduled to go to Berlin, then transfer to Denmark, study for a week, and then return to Germany.

Jiangsu Province Sends Personnel to Supervise the Collection of Education Funds 81

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Funding Management Office, because the province's education funds have been designated as taxes from teeth traders and slaughterhouses, to be collected and remitted as much as possible. There is a clear distinction between these funds and other government expenses. However, because the land tax is collected as a whole, the dedicated education funds are not separated and stored separately at the time of collection. There is only the name of separation, but no responsibility for it, and it has become common practice to divert and advance funds. Recently, it was found that the amount of arrears owed by various counties is increasing year by year, and the provincial and departmental education funds are in a precarious state. Therefore, it is planned to send capable personnel to various counties to discuss and settle the matter, so that the dedicated funds collected each day will be directly drawn from the grain treasury, designated collection agencies will be established, and funds will be stored separately. They will still be jointly submitted by the resident supervising committee on a monthly basis, in order to fundamentally solve the problem. Fearing that the counties would shirk responsibility, a public letter was sent to the provincial government, ordering all counties to comply. The magistrate of Wuxi County, Chen, has also received orders to comply.

Ministry of Education Orders Shandong University to Give Preferential Treatment to Mongolian and Tibetan Students 82

In order to promote Mongolian and Tibetan education, the Ministry of Education previously ordered Peking University and National Central University to each establish Mongolian and Tibetan specialty classes, and at the same time stipulated measures to give preferential treatment to Mongolian and Tibetan students, and issued notices to all universities to comply. Now, the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission has requested that Shandong University be instructed to admit Mongolian student Huang Wenxiang to study in accordance with the regulations for treating Mongolian and Tibetan students. In addition to replying to the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, Shandong University was also instructed to admit Mongolian students and handle the matter in accordance with the regulations for treatment.

Huaiyin Normal School Convenes Education Conference for Nine Counties 83

Qingjiangpu, 30th dispatch. Gu Kangbo, the principal of the provincial Huaiyin Normal School, convened education personnel from the nine counties of Weihuai, Liansi, Musu, Fugao, and Bao on the 28th to discuss the improvement of education in the region. A total of 55 proposals were submitted, and 31 were passed. The meeting closed today.

Hard Court Tennis Tournament, Yu Tianguang Shows Promise 98

▲Defeated Strong Enemy Shi Guiya Yesterday

▲Liang Deguang Defeated Crawford

▲The Two Will Compete for the Final

The Hard Court Tennis Championship organized by the French Chamber of Commerce was in its second day yesterday. In the men's singles, the interest was concentrated on the group of Yu Tianguang vs. Shi Guiya. Shi is a strong player from the American community, and it was difficult to distinguish between Yu and him. As a result, Yu won the right to the second round with a score of 7-5, 4-6, 6-2. At the same time, in another group, Liang Deguang won the right to the second round with a score of 6-1, 6-0 against Crawford. Yu Liang will meet in the second round. The competition will continue from Saturday.

▲Yu Tianguang's victory over Shi Guiya, the victory or defeat of the two depends entirely on the level. Both sides fought with long strokes, but Yu's shots were hard and powerful. Shi touched the net a lot. Yu also gathered all his strength and finally defeated the enemy. In the first set, Yu won two games with a clean four-game winning streak, and then Shi got two games, four to two, and then four to four. Yu won five to four, and Shi leveled again. Yu finally won the first set with seven to five. In the second set, Shi led with four to two and five to three, and made it one to one with six to four. In the third set to determine the victory or defeat, Shi took the lead with two to one, but lost five games in a row and was defeated by a score of six to two.

▲Liang Deguang's victory over Crawford, Crawford was not a strong opponent of Liang. In the two sets, Crawford only won one game, six to one, six to zero, completed in twenty minutes.

▲The situation of the men's singles, at the moment, there is a trend that Chinese people will monopolize the singles. Yu Tianguang, Liang Deguang, and Sun Linfang have all entered the second round. The other one is none other than Bellings. In the Yu Liang second round, Sun will play the fourth person in the second round. Based on past achievements, Yu Tianguang has the most hope of winning the championship. ▲There is fierce competition in doubles. Among the doubles, the four strongest teams are: (1) Zheng Zhaojia and Jiang Daozhang, (2) Shi Guiya and Shi Misi, (2) Canafanvalo and Tafolasi, (4) Bellings and Meyers. Inter-Port Trial Match Record 101

—Zhou Xianyan Team Wins 5-2—

—The Performance of the Chinese Players Was Very Outstanding—

The Shanghai Port Team Football Team held its first trial match at Yiyuan at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. There were about 10,000 spectators, which was a great event. As a result, Zhou Xianyan's team defeated Gaxu's team 5-2. Both teams performed well, and the interest was strong. All the skills were fully demonstrated. I am very satisfied with the appreciation. The process is recorded as follows

(1) Brief Description of Football Skills 102

▲Zhou Xianyan Team Zhou's left inside forward Turner did not play.

Chen Hongguang from Donghua replaced him. The forwards of this team did not seem to be as sharp as those of Gaxu. However, yesterday's performance was completely different. The shooting was almost good, and the connection was also wonderful. Especially Chen Jiaqiu's ferrying in all directions was the most effective. Laudon and Chen Hongguang also reached the top. The most sophisticated were the defenders. Zhou Xianyan's goalkeeper need not be criticized again. Li Ning and Feng Yundong, the two inside defenders, were as solid as iron, unbreakable, well-positioned, and controlled. The ideal Gaxu team forwards could not cross the Leichi line. On the central defender side, Xu Yahui was the most prominent, running all over the field, taking care of all directions, and responding in all directions. His skills were far above those of Gaxu. He was the most prominent of the three with Li and Feng yesterday. Right winger Huisiwu was also very commendable, followed by Madaci. In short, Zhou's defense was far above that of Gaxu. It was no accident that they won 5-2.

▲Gaxu Team Gaxu's performance was unexpected. In the first quarter of an hour after the start, they were very brave. The forwards pressed Zhou's team tightly, making Zhou Xianyan busy with rescue. Fortunately, they did not lose. But from then on, they were at a loss, and Chen Rong was scattered, making it difficult to peep. In addition, Zhou's team had a tight defense, which was impeccable. Li Yichen's performance was quite regressive compared to before, and his actions were slow and his feet were inaccurate. The biggest problem was that he could not cooperate with others, so Li did not see any outstanding performance yesterday. Chen Zhenhe often had the impression of isolated applause. The defenders were far inferior to Zhou's team, and there were no outstanding performances.

(2) Competition Process 103

▲First Ball Gaxu team kicked off and attacked fiercely. The forwards were very brave. Zhou Xianyan belonged to the brink of danger, punching and kicking. Fortunately, the frame was raised properly, and the dragon gate was preserved. After twenty minutes, Zhou's team sent troops to attack, Jiaqiu Hongguang and Laudon fought in close quarters, broke through the defense line, Laudon succeeded in one fell swoop, very clear and powerful.

▲Second Ball Gaxu team was kicked in front of the goal for a free kick. Zhou's team Xu Yahui kicked very well. Goalkeeper David saved it. After this wave was flat, five or six minutes later, Zhou's team made a comeback. Laudon went on a rampage and broke the dragon gate again, making it two to zero. This is the result of the first half

▲Third Ball About three minutes after the start of the second half, Zhou's right winger Fafan timidly reached the bottom line, and sent the ball to the center, Gaxu's front gate, quite a desolate scene, Chen Hongguang headed the ball properly, and the header entered the door, the situation was very beautiful, making it three to zero

▲Fourth Ball This ball was also headed in by Chen Hongguang, thanks to Chen Jiaqiu's remote transfer, Hongguang can be said to be good at using his head, the ball's entry, only two or three minutes away from the third ball

▲Fifth Ball After Zhou's team won the fourth ball, Gaxu's team kicked off in the center, and went all the way down, Chen Zhenhe, Li Yichen, Burns, shoulder to shoulder, directly into the enemy camp, after a considerable amount of time, Chen Zhenhe attacked the goal, and the ball entered the net, Gaxu's team then recorded, making it one to four

▲Sixth Ball Zhou's right winger Huisiwu, kicked a free kick against Gaxu's goal. The ball flew to the front of the goal. Laudon headed it, and the ball went to the right. David wanted to save it but failed, and the ball was obtained by Chen Jiaqiu, who shot it quickly, making it five to one.

▲Seventh Ball Suddenly saw Li Ning injured in the ear, Zhou Xianyan could not pay attention to the situation of the ball because of taking care of Li, so the interior was empty, and the Dragon Gate was shaken, Gaxu team Li Yichen dribbled in and succeeded in one fell swoop, sending the result to five to two, Zhou Jiayan team won

(III) Reflections on Watching the Game 104

Yesterday was only the first trial match, and the official lineup is still difficult to determine. It will take a second or third rehearsal before a decision can be made. The gentlemen in charge have their own insightful views on selecting talent. Here, I will briefly describe what the reporter observed yesterday:

▲ Goalkeeper and Inner Defense: In the goalkeeper battle, Zhou Xianyan is unmatched in Shanghai. There is no doubt that he should be selected as the official player. In terms of inner defense, Li Ning and Feng Yunyou are capable and handle things properly, without any flaws. Based on yesterday's observations, Li and Feng are also the only candidates for the official team.

▲ Midfield Talent: The most difficult problem in midfield is Xu Yahui and Gan Xu. Gan Xu serves as the captain of the trial matches and has been the captain of the Shanghai Port team in previous years. It is inevitable that he will be selected as the center midfielder. However, this gentleman has not performed well in any of the previous competitions this year, and yesterday was no exception. On the other hand, Xu Yahui, who came to Shanghai from Malaya, is currently the leading midfielder in Shanghai, rarely surpassed. His performances yesterday and in the past have been outstanding, unmatched by Gan Xu. There is a real possibility that he will be selected for the important position of official center midfielder. However, Gan Xu has higher seniority and is related to the reputation of Westerners. Although his skills cannot surpass Xu, it is difficult for Xu to seize Gan Xu's position. If they have to settle for second best, Xu might be used as the left or right midfielder. As for the other midfielder, Whiswood seems to have the highest chance of being selected.

▲ Forward Lineup: The forward lineup is difficult to arrange. Looking at yesterday's situation, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Zhenhe, Chen Hongguang, and Lawton were the best, followed by Fafanqie, Alger, Wan Xianghua. Wan is short and weak, making it difficult for him to cope with strong opponents. Fafanqie was the best winger yesterday, but his footwork is a bit slow, which is a pity. With the above talents, Lawton can be the center forward, Hongguang can be the left inside, Jiaqiu can be the right inside, Zhenhe can be the left winger, and Fafanqie can be the right winger. If Li Yichen can use all his energy to achieve good results in the second trial match, it is not difficult for him to be selected.

The above is just the reporter's humble opinion and may not be appreciated by knowledgeable people. This matter is important, and the selection committee has its own insightful views and will arrange the most complete and strongest lineup. Yesterday's lineup was as follows:

Mr. Wang did not land due to illness and continued his voyage to Europe for medical treatment on the original ship. After arriving in Hong Kong, Mr. Zeng stayed briefly and then returned to Shanghai on the French postal ship Mesange. The ship docked at the China Merchants Bureau's Central Wharf at around 11:00 AM yesterday morning. Mrs. Zeng Zhongming, Ms. Fang Junbi, and others were there to welcome him. After landing, he went directly to Wang's residence on Xipu Shilu to rest. Mr. Zeng is scheduled to go to Beijing by night train tonight. Mr. Zeng's conversation with a reporter from the Central News Agency on the ship is recorded below:

▲ Wang Arrived in Saigon: According to Mr. Zeng, Mr. Wang took a three-month leave from the central government to go to Europe for treatment due to a tropical disease. When the ship passed through Hong Kong, he also did not land due to illness, but only met with Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, and other representatives on the ship. He himself could not send him far due to official duties, so he landed in Hong Kong and returned to Shanghai on this ship.
